1. Intelligence develops that Lucia von Bardas, post-coup Latverian government, is funding U.S.-based supervillain technological proliferation as deniable asymmetric retaliation for prior American interference in Latverian affairs.
2. Subject presents intelligence to the President / Council. Response is institutionally inadequate by the subject's assessment — formal diplomatic channels, sanctions framework, no kinetic option.
3. Subject privately determines kinetic option is required.
4. Subject assembles a black-operations team of superhuman contractors — Captain America, Wolverine, Spider-Man, Daredevil, Luke Cage, Black Widow, others — under **partial and misleading briefings**. Participants are not told the operation is unsanctioned; not told the political stakes; not told the foreseeable blowback.
5. Operation executes. Von Bardas's government is decapitated. Subject vanishes the team's memory of the operation through pharmacological/technological means.
6. Twelve months later, the blowback (Latverian-funded coordinated U.S.-based supervillain attacks on the unwitting participants) lands. People nearly die. The truth of the original operation surfaces.
7. Subject is exposed, formally removed from directorship, goes AWOL.

The behavioral significance is total. **This is the canonical rupture point** — the moment the subject crosses from "uses ugly means for sanctioned ends" to "uses uglier means for ends he alone has sanctioned, against allies he has lied to, and disappears rather than account for it."

Granular behavioral observations from the depicted sequence:

- The subject **briefs each participant individually**, not collectively. This is tradecraft, but it is also affective avoidance — he does not have to face the group registering, in concert, what they are being asked to do.
- The subject's affect in the briefing scenes is **softer** than his operational baseline. He is solicitous. He is using the relational capital of every prior shared operation. This is the manipulative register he has avoided across most of the record; deployed here, it is recognizable as a defense against his own awareness of what he is doing.
- The post-operation memory intervention is the **single most significant violation of consent in the depicted record**, and the subject performs it without on-panel hesitation. The defense structure has fully closed; the omnipotent-control / messianic rationalization findings of Section 3 are evidenced in operational form here for the first time at this scale.
- The AWOL — the immediate exfiltration to deep cover when exposed — is not panicked. It is prepared. **The subject had the escape plan in place before the operation. He had always had the escape plan in place.** This is the operational manifestation of the foundational pattern noted in Section I: *every institution he enters, he enters with a pre-negotiated exit.*

The relational cost is the cost the subject is least equipped to metabolize. Captain America in particular — the closest thing to a peer the subject has had outside the Commandos — does not forgive in any timeframe depicted by the canon. The Avengers as an institution will not work with him under his own name for the remainder of the period covered by this section. **The subject has, in a single operational sequence, severed the entire upper register of his peer relationships, the relationships he has been depending on for decades to anchor what is left of his moral self-concept.**

He absorbs this cost with the same flatness with which he has absorbed every prior cost.

---

## VIII. Cumulative Pattern Evolution Across the Middle Period

Read end to end, the middle period is the documented arc of a single behavioral process operating across forty years:

- **The perimeter of decisions reserved to the subject alone widens, monotonically, in every depicted crisis.** From "this operation, my call" (Howling Commandos) to "this agency, my call" (Steranko) to "this agency's existence, my call" (Deltite) to "this nation-state's government, my call" (Secret War).
- **The number of people the subject confides in fully contracts, monotonically.** From the squad (seven) to the inner circle (Dugan, Val, Jones — three) to the operational confidants of the late directorship (Dugan, possibly one or two others) to, by the AWOL period, effectively no one.
- **The defenses harden.** Compartmentalization moves from skill to method to personality to ontology. Isolation of affect deepens. Identification with the aggressor advances visibly across the decades — the subject of 2004 uses methods the subject of 1968 would have refused, and uses them on people the subject of 1968 would have died for.
- **The somatic baseline remains, impossibly, intact.** Conditioning maintained. Field competence preserved. Cigar, patch, profanity, posture — the visual grammar of the man is unchanged across forty years of publication. The body has not registered what the psychology has absorbed. This is itself a clinical finding: the **somatization-by-non-somatization** of a trauma load that has nowhere else to go and is being held entirely by character armor.
- **The capacity for romantic intimacy attenuates to nil.** Hawley (loss, 1940s). Defabio (abandonment, 1950s). Val (slow dissolution, 1970s–1990s). After Val, in the depicted record, **nothing**. The subject is, by the end of the middle period, a man who has not been intimately known by another human being in any sustained way for the better part of a generation, and who has organized his life to make sure this remains the case.
- **The capacity for mentorship intensifies as the capacity for peerage degrades.** The cultivation of Coulson, Johnson, and the broader successor generation is the displacement object of all the affective investment the subject can no longer route through his peer and romantic relationships. He cannot say what people mean to him; he can assign them to the operations that will mean their lives.

The middle period closes with the subject exfiltrated, off-grid, under indictment in all but name, with the institutional life he constructed dissolving behind him and the apparatus he will need for the next phase — the off-book Caterpillar program, the parallel intelligence service, the Hickman-era findings — already in his possession.

He has, by 2004, become a man who can only operate alone, who has built the conditions of his isolation himself, and who experiences those conditions as the proof of his necessity.

The next section will document the underground period and the discovery that the apparatus he was running was always a smaller, secret duplicate of the one he was being lied to inside of — and the subject's response, which is not collapse, but escalation.


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — RECENT HISTORY & CURRENT STATE

*Subject: Fury, N.J. (Sr.) — Operational Status: Anomalous / Extraterrestrial-Bound / Intermittent Re-Entry*

---

## 4.1 — The Hinge Years (Bendis era closeout, c. 2008–2012): From Director to Fugitive to Architect

The decade leading into the subject's current condition begins with the **Skrull Secret Invasion** (Bendis, 2008). Subject — already off-book since the Latverian rupture of 2004 — re-emerges from underground precisely at the moment his vindication is unanswerable: every institution that disowned him after Secret War (the National Security Council, the post-Maria Hill S.H.I.E.L.D., the Avengers leadership) has been demonstrably penetrated by infiltrators he alone had been hunting. He surfaces leading a hand-picked, deeply compartmentalized cell — the **Secret Warriors / "Caterpillars"** — children of superhumans whose existence he had been quietly cataloguing for years against precisely this contingency. Behavioral signature of this period: he does not return triumphant; he returns **briefly, transactionally, and exits the frame the instant the immediate threat is contained.** No interest in restored title. No interest in apology owed. He had already grieved the institution.

The **Norman Osborn / Dark Reign interval (2008–2010)** finds him operating entirely subterranean, with the Caterpillars partitioned into cells (Gorgon, Druid, Hellfire, Stonewall, Phobos, Yo-Yo, Quake) that did not know of each other until tactical necessity forced disclosure. The **Hickman *Secret Warriors* run (2009–2011)** is the period's defining text and the most painful single revelation in the subject's biography: that **S.H.I.E.L.D. itself was a HYDRA front from inception**, that **Baron Strucker had been running Fury's chain of command for sixty in-world years**, and that the agency the subject built — believed he built — had been a containment apparatus *for him* as much as a tool *of* him. He receives this intelligence and does not visibly decompensate. He proceeds to dismantle HYDRA in a methodical extermination campaign that costs him **most of the Caterpillars** (Gorgon, Hellfire's defection and death, the catastrophic Phobos sacrifice — a twelve-year-old boy, the son of Ares, gunned down by Strucker after refusing to kneel). The Phobos death is operationally pivotal: the subject's compartmentalization permitted him to deploy a child as a war-asset, and the child died on principle the subject himself authored. There is **no canonical depiction of the subject mourning Phobos**. There is a canonical depiction of him handing the boy's body off and walking back to operations within the page. This is the most legible single instance of the subject's late-period **isolation of affect** in the published record.

Coming out of Hickman, the subject is approximately as alone as he has ever been. Dugan present. Val gone (long since). Jones present but aging. Daisy Johnson elevated to Directorship of the reconstituted S.H.I.E.L.D. as the subject's chosen successor — and then almost immediately displaced. The pattern of the period: **the subject grooms successors and then is structurally unable to ratify their authority**, because no authority but his own meets his standard.

## 4.2 — The Son (2012): Editorial Rejuvenation and the Father-Repetition

In 2012, Marvel introduced **Nicholas J. Fury Jr.** — an Army Ranger, biracial, monocular by combat injury, designed transparently to repatriate the comics character to the screen persona then ascendant. The in-universe mechanism: a son the subject had not raised, by **Nia Jones, sister of Gabriel Jones**. The subject's reaction in canon to the discovery and integration of his adult son is **the single most diagnostic family scene in the entire record**: he does not embrace, does not apologize, does not explain. He briefs. He extends operational trust before he extends paternal acknowledgment. He places the son inside the work because the work is the only place he knows how to place a person he values.

**This is the absent-pilot-father template the subject inherited from his own childhood, executed identically across a generational gap.** He has become the man whose absence formed him. The published record contains no scene of the two Furys at a domestic table, no shared meal, no inquiry by the elder into the younger's life prior to service. The younger Fury occupies the role of *capable subordinate the elder cannot bring himself to call son out loud.* When the elder is later removed from the board (see §4.3), the younger inherits the eyepatch, the trench coat, and the public-facing name — but not the depth of the network, the Formula, or the relationship.

## 4.3 — *Original Sin* (Aaron, 2014): The Watcher's Murder and the Sentence

The **Watcher Uatu** is found dead on the lunar surface, eyes excised. The investigation occupies the entire summer event of 2014 and culminates in a triple revelation:

1. **The subject killed Uatu.** Not in malice — in mercy and necessity, after Uatu was mortally wounded by another party, and to prevent the cosmic intelligence in the eyes from falling fully into hostile hands. The lethal blow is the subject's.
2. **The subject has been operating, for an unknown but multi-decade duration, as "The Man on the Wall"** — a hereditary, off-the-books planetary defense post passed down outside any government's knowledge, whose holder is authorized to preemptively assassinate threats Earth does not yet know exist. The subject inherited the position quietly. He has used it.
3. **The Infinity Formula has been failing.** The body the subject has been wearing through the late period is a vigorously maintained illusion; underneath, accelerated aging has been advancing. The "Fury" the public saw at *Original Sin* — coat, patch, cigar — was a **performance maintained over a desiccating substrate.**

In the issue's closing pages the subject is shown as he physiologically *is*: ancient, withered, skeletal, still upright. The Watchers' tribunal does not execute him. They **sentence him to replace what he destroyed.** He is bound to the Moon, transfigured into **"The Unseen"** — perception expanded to Watcher-grade, mobility eliminated, intervention prohibited.

**This is the canonical endpoint already reached.** The man whose identity is action is iatrogenically immobilized into pure witness. The cigar is gone. The trench is gone. The patch is irrelevant; both eyes are open now and they see everything they should not.

## 4.4 — The Unseen Period (2014–c. 2018): The Sentence Endured

The subject's published appearances during this period are sparse, deliberately so. He appears principally in:

- **The remainder of *Original Sin* and its tie-ins**, dispensing fragments of withheld history to a small number of characters as currency-of-last-resort. He weaponizes his new omniscience the way he used to weaponize files.
- **Brief lunar visits across the line** — Star-Lord, the Avengers, an interrogation by Doctor Strange — in which he is **physically static, vocally diminished, expressively still recognizable**: the dry register, the refusal to flatter, the unbroken willingness to deliver information the listener will hate.
- **The Ewing *Ultimates*² lunar conference** in which cosmic-tier operators consult him about deep-time threats.

Behavioral data extractable from the period despite reduced screen time:

- **He does not beg for release.** Across multiple writers, the subject treats the sentence as just. He killed Uatu; he accepts what followed. The OCPD-spectrum moral overcontrol holds.
- **He attempts to keep operating.** Confined to perception, he runs intelligence operations *via what he tells whom*. He selects auditors based on long-cultivated reads of their character. He still mentors — Bucky Barnes, the Winter Soldier, is one notable late-period auditor he selects for delicate disclosures.
- **The compartmentalization remains intact.** Even as Watcher-analog with near-omniscient field, he discloses fragments, not totalities. Even sentenced to total witness, he chooses what others may see.
- **The grief he could not metabolize across a century becomes ambient.** Multiple writers depict him watching specific persons (Dugan; the son; Daisy) without intervening, with an expression that does not appear elsewhere in his record. This is the subject *registering*, finally, with no permitted action, what he had been unable to register while there was always one more operation.

The Unseen period is — clinically read — **enforced exposure therapy administered to a man who would never have undergone it voluntarily.** The therapeutic value is unmeasurable and unwitnessed. The cost in identity is severe.

## 4.5 — Re-Entry and Operational Restoration (c. 2018–present): Earth-Bound Again

Across the late 2010s into the 2020s the subject is **incrementally restored to terrestrial operation** — the exact mechanism varies by writer (a successor Watcher arrangement; the Formula stabilized in restored form; the sentence commuted or completed) but the in-canon facts are: the subject walks Earth again. The patch is back. The cigar is back. The trench is back. The body presents as a man in late middle age once more.

But he is not the man who left.

**Documented changes, recent canon:**

- **He is operating at lower public visibility than at any previous point in his career.** He does not seek the Directorship. He has no interest in S.H.I.E.L.D.'s perennial reorganizations (the agency itself has collapsed and re-formed under various names — S.H.I.E.L.D., S.W.O.R.D. under Abigail Brand, off-book equivalents — and he ratifies none of them by joining). He is, functionally, **a freelance asset of himself.**
- **He moves through the global theater laterally** — appearances in Madripoor, in Krakoan-adjacent intelligence work during the mutant nation's existence, in the Wakandan diplomatic shadow-channels, in the contested no-man's-land of post-*Devil's Reign* New York. He is a known quantity to every intelligence apparatus on Earth and accountable to none of them.
- **His network is curated to perhaps a dozen names.** Dugan (still alive, similarly Formula-extended). Gabe Jones (depending on writer-state, often deceased, occasionally still extant in deep retirement). Daisy Johnson. Phil Coulson (status unstable through the *Devil's Reign* corruption arc). Maria Hill (deceased — *Hickman/Gillen Avengers*, *Hellfire Gala* fallout; the subject's reaction has not been textualized at the depth the loss warrants and that absence is itself diagnostic). The son. A handful of ex-Caterpillars (Yo-Yo, Quake). **He has not added a new intimate to the circle in over a decade of in-universe time.**
- **He is, by his own implicit operating doctrine, semi-retired from sovereignty** — the "Man on the Wall" function is canonically dispersed/restructured post-*Original Sin*. He still acts unilaterally when the moment demands; he no longer maintains the standing infrastructure to act unilaterally as a default mode. This is the closest thing to a course correction visible in the longitudinal record.

## 4.6 — Current Somatic and Behavioral State

**Body.** Re-stabilized Formula. Physiologically presenting in the conditioned late-40s baseline that has been the canonical appearance since the 1960s. Monocular as ever; patch refused-prosthesis as ever. The skeletal Unseen substrate revealed in *Original Sin* is now sub-dermal — known to him to be the truth beneath the presentation. **He knows what he looks like under the Formula in a way he did not know before 2014.** This is a permanent alteration in self-perception even when external appearance is restored.

**Cigar.** Restored. The ritual function intact: paced breath, oral self-regulation, occupational tell.

**Sleep.** No domestic environment on record. Operational sleep, transit sleep, safehouse sleep. The pattern of seven decades persists.

**Affect.** Slightly — *slightly* — less constricted than in the immediate pre-*Original Sin* period. Multiple recent writers have permitted a dry warmth in scenes with Daisy, with the son, with Bucky, that the Bendis-era subject would have edited out. The Unseen tenure appears to have produced a small and grudging concession: that being seen is not solely a tactical liability.

**Cognition.** Pattern-recognition undegraded. Strategic horizon still measured in decades. **Newly: a willingness to share intelligence with successors at a depth he previously refused** — an operational legacy posture consistent with a man who has now experienced the prospect of being permanently removed from the board and has decided that some of what he knows must outlive him.

## 4.7 — Where He Is Now

Geographic: **untraceable as a matter of professional discipline.** Pattern-of-life data points to repeated cycling among approximately a dozen safehouses across three continents, with periodic lunar visits (whether nostalgic, operational, or ceremonial is unclear and likely all three). New York presence is intermittent and routed through dead-drops, not residence. He maintains no public address, no published telephony, no biometric registration with any state.

Institutional: **affiliated with no agency.** Wary collegial relations with S.W.O.R.D. (Brand), with Wakandan intelligence (Okoye-era and successor), with the surviving Avengers leadership. Acrimonious-but-functional relations with whatever the current S.H.I.E.L.D.-successor formation is on any given week. He is consulted; he does not report.

Relational: **circle at historical minimum, depth at historical maximum within that minimum.** The handful who remain have been with him for in-universe lifetimes. Loss of any one would, per the established pressure-point map, **bypass every defense** — and the actuarial pressure on that small circle increases every year, even with the Formula extending Dugan.

Existential: **a man who has been sentenced, served, and returned, and who knows that the role he resumed is the one that earned the sentence.** There is no canonical scene in which he articulates an intention to change. There is no canonical scene in which he behaves as if he believes change is possible. There is, scattered across the post-2018 record, a quieter quality — a willingness to let conversations end without a tactical payoff, a willingness to let a former subordinate run an operation he would once have run himself, a willingness to mentor the son in fragments — that suggests something the subject would never name and might not himself recognize: **the beginnings, three-quarters of a century late, of grief permitted to happen.**

He is, in the present tense of the published record:

- biologically forty-something, chronologically post-centenarian, ontologically uncertain;
- operationally active, institutionally unaffiliated, personally uncatalogued;
- still cigar, still patch, still trench;
- still the man who does what others won't;
- still — and this is the line beneath every other line in this file — **the only person he has ever fully trusted with the decisions he has made**, and increasingly aware, in a way he was not at the height of his sovereignty, of what that cost has been.

The trajectory from here is short. The Formula will fail again or it will not. The small circle will contract again or it will not. The next catastrophe will arrive on schedule. He will be where it is. He will not be invited. He will not wait to be.

That is the current state. That is where he is. That is how he got here.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 2: MEDICAL HISTORY

**Subject:** Fury, Nicholas Joseph (Sr.)
**File reference:** Somatic record, longitudinal — chronological 1920s–present; biological apparent age ~45 throughout post-1945 record.
**Compiler's note:** What follows is not a chart in the clinical sense; it is the body considered as document. Every scar on Fury is also a sentence in a longer paragraph about who he chose to be in the moment the iron entered him. Treat accordingly.

---

## 2.1 Constitutional Baseline — Pre-Service (c. 1920–1940)

The pre-war pediatric and adolescent record is, predictably, sparse. The subject was born to working-class Irish-American parents in Hell's Kitchen, Manhattan, in the interwar period (canonical date variable; Infinity Formula complicates linear reckoning). Father — Jack Fury, WWI aviator — was killed in service; subject grew up in the somatic culture of Depression-era tenement New York, which is to say: bare-knuckle settling of grievances on stairwells and sidewalks, undertreated childhood infections, dental neglect, and the kind of nutritional baseline that produces wiry, dense, durable men with low body-fat percentages and excellent grip strength into late life.

By apparent adolescence the subject was an established street fighter (referenced retroactively in *Fury* GN, 1994, and *Fury: Peacemaker*). Knuckles of both hands show old, well-healed metacarpal microtrauma consistent with years of bare-knuckle striking — the boxer's hands. Nasal bridge has been broken at least twice prior to enlistment; a slight rightward deviation of the septum is visible across artists and decades. He has chronic mild snoring referenced in shared-quarters scenes (*Sgt. Fury* run, Howlers in barracks); the septal deformity is the likely mechanism.

No documented surgical history pre-enlistment. No documented immunizations beyond Army-standard. Dental: pre-enlistment dentition shows posterior decay typical of cohort; later military dentistry catches him up. He carries one gold-crowned molar (upper right second molar) visible in close-quarters art, vintage interbellum work.

**Inference:** the subject entered adult service with a body already pre-shaped for impact. He has never known a body that wasn't taking damage. This is foundational.

---

## 2.2 World War II — Formative Trauma Load (1941–1945)

The Howling Commandos period is the densest somatic-injury window of the entire record and the period in which the body Fury still walks around in was, essentially, *case-hardened*.

**Cumulative documented injuries, WWII theater (Sgt. Fury #1–#167, retrospectives, and *Fury Files*):**

- Multiple gunshot wounds (left thigh, right shoulder, left flank — through-and-through, 1943; right deltoid GSW, North Africa; left forearm graze, Italy). At least one GSW (flank) developed mild wound infection; pre-penicillin-availability sulfonamide treatment in field; left a puckered, depigmented scar approximately 4 cm.
- Shrapnel: distributed across posterior torso, both thighs, left hand. Several fragments judged surgically unsafe to extract and left in situ; these have been an intermittent issue on metal detectors and an absolute issue at the MRI suite throughout the modern era. Field medics in 1944 noted retained fragments at L3–L4 paraspinous musculature; these have produced episodic low back pain (referenced in body-language, occasional palm-to-lumbar in Steranko-era art).
- Concussive injury: multiple, undocumented because field-undocumented. The grenade blast that took the eye also produced a closed-head injury with brief LOC and almost certain mild TBI. There were earlier and later events of the same class. **Cumulative subconcussive load over WWII alone exceeds modern football-cohort thresholds for delayed neurodegenerative risk.** The Infinity Formula appears to confer some protection here, on the available evidence; absent it, the subject's modern cognitive profile would not be possible.
- **The eye. France, 1944 (*Sgt. Fury* #27, 1966).** Penetrating ocular trauma from grenade fragmentation. Globe rupture, enucleation performed in field/aid station conditions. **No prosthesis.** The orbital socket has healed cleanly; tissue around the rim shows fine radial scarring consistent with the original blast pattern (visible when the patch is removed in rare canonical instances — Steranko, *Strange Tales*; Hitch, *Ultimates*; Aaron, *Original Sin*). Lid function on the affected side is partial; he can blink-cover but the lid sits high without the patch.
  - **The medical decision-tree, then and after:** by the 1970s, prosthetic eye technology — cosmetic shells, magnetic-mounted prostheses, eventually limited bionic substitution — was canonically available to him through S.H.I.E.L.D. medical and refused at every offering. The refusal is on the record. He has stated, when pressed by Dugan and others, variants of "I earned it." **This is not a medical fact. It is a psychological monument that happens to involve a missing organ.** See §3.
  - **Functional sequelae:** monocular vision with complete loss of stereopsis on the left field, requiring constant head-turning compensation (visible across every artist from Kirby to Deodato — Fury rarely sits squared to anyone; he sits at ~15–20° rotation to maximize right-field coverage and keep the patch toward the wall). Compensatory cervical strain over decades; he carries tension at the right trapezius and suboccipital region. He occupies elevated and corner positions in rooms reflexively. He hates being addressed from the left and will physically reposition rather than turn his head every time.
- Fractures: left clavicle (parachute landing, behind lines, 1943); right 6th and 7th ribs (twice — once 1942 hand-to-hand, once 1944 fall); right ulnar styloid (close-quarters, no date); both hands carry old boxer's fractures of the 5th metacarpal. None set under ideal conditions; all healed with mild deformity that does not impair function.
- Burns: second-degree flash burns to dorsal right forearm and right cheek/neck, 1944 — incendiary device incident. The right neck burn is small but visible in raking light; the forearm burn is hairless in a 6 cm patch.
- Hypothermia (Ardennes, winter 1944) — survived; no permanent peripheral neuropathy on the record, though intermittent cold-sensitivity in extremities is consistent.
- Near-drowning (Channel insertion gone wrong, 1943) — survived without ARDS-equivalent complication.
- Foreign-body insults: chemical exposure to HYDRA prototype agents in late-war operations (precise compounds redacted from any record I can construct); no acute toxidrome documented; possible chronic exposure significance unknown.

**The WWII period as somatic baseline:** by VE-day Fury had a body that had been broken in approximately a dozen specific ways and rebuilt in approximately a dozen specific compromises. He emerged with: monocular vision, retained shrapnel, multiple healed fractures, a pre-existing tinnitus (artillery exposure) that he has now lived with for the entire chronological remainder of his life, and the somatic conviction that pain is a piece of information rather than a problem.

---

## 2.3 The Infinity Formula — The Iatrogenic Spine of Everything After

**Event:** Late 1944/early 1945, France. Severe abdominal-and-thoracic blast trauma, exsanguinating, ferried by partisan network to the laboratory of **Dr. Berthold Sternberg** (*Marvel Spotlight* #31, 1976; Wolfman/Friedrich elaboration; revisited Ennis, *Fury* MAX, 2001–2002).

**Intervention:** Administration of the experimental compound subsequently designated the Infinity Formula. Acute effect: survival when survival was not medically expected. Chronic effect: arrest of biological aging at approximately the apparent age of administration (mid-40s phenotype), maintained indefinitely *conditional on annual booster*. Without booster, the suppressed chronological aging decompensates rapidly and catastrophically — the body attempts to "catch up" across decades over a span of weeks.

**Mechanism (in-universe, partial):** unknown to subject; partially understood by Sternberg, who weaponized this asymmetry by extracting payments and concessions for decades. After Sternberg's death the formula became a controlled, scarce resource — synthesizable by a small handful of biochemists who Fury has, across the record, variously protected, employed, threatened, or kidnapped.

**Confirmed shared recipients:** Timothy "Dum Dum" Dugan (the durability of the Fury–Dugan dyad across the modern record is medically as well as emotionally founded — they are the only two men in each other's lives who do not age out). A handful of other operational intimates have been dosed in fragments or attempts, with mixed results.

**Somatic effects beyond age-arrest:**
- Modestly accelerated baseline wound healing — not superhuman, but at the high end of human plasticity. A laceration that would heal in 10 days in a fit civilian heals in 6–7 in Fury.
- Resistance to certain neurodegenerative processes (inferred — see TBI load above; he is cognitively intact at chronological 100+).
- Possible immunomodulation — he has not been documented seriously ill from infectious disease in the post-1945 record, despite austere environments.
- **No conferred strength, speed, or sensory enhancement.** Baseline elite human, maintained by training.

**Psychological impact of the Formula** — this is properly §3 material but must be flagged here because the medical fact *generates* the psychology:
1. **Pharmacological leash.** Annual dependency on a substance produced by a finite, mortal supplier network. Fury has organized portions of his life around supply security in the manner of a chronically ill person who must travel with insulin into unstable regions — except his "insulin" is hunted by HYDRA, by hostile intelligence services, and by would-be inheritors. He has tortured for it (Ennis). He has killed for it. He does not discuss it.
2. **Stacked bereavement.** He has now buried, by my estimate from canon, on the order of dozens of people he loved without aging the corresponding number of years himself. Every funeral has been an out-of-phase event. The body that attends them is the body that was 45 in 1945. **The grief has no chronological architecture to settle into.** See §3 — Prolonged Grief.
3. **Survivor signature.** The Formula has converted survivor's guilt into a permanent metabolic state. He did not survive one event; he is surviving every event, continuously, by design.
4. **Temporal vertigo.** Operationally he plans in decades. Domestically he cannot, because the people in domestic frames are on human clocks. This produces a documented behavioral pattern of withdrawal from intimate timelines.

**Dependency profile:** medically iatrogenic, volitionally non-voluntary, psychologically experienced as a leash. Not a substance use disorder in the DSM sense. Functionally indistinguishable from one in his felt experience.

---

## 2.4 Cold War / Korea / Indochina — The Middle Decades of Accumulation (c. 1946–1965)

This period (canonically densest in Ennis, *Fury: My War Gone By*, 2012; *Peacemaker*; the *Howling Commandos of S.H.I.E.L.D.* retrospectives) is the era in which the Formula's protective signature becomes visible and in which the somatic record begins to diverge from a normal-mortal trajectory.

**Documented somatic events, this period:**
- Multiple additional GSWs (Korea, Indochina, Cuba, Congo). Cumulative GSW count across the full record is conservatively in the high twenties.
- Malaria, contracted Indochina, treated with quinine and chloroquine; recurrent low-grade febrile episodes for years after, eventually quiescent. Possibly cleared by Formula-mediated immune effect.
- Hepatitis (type unspecified, almost certainly A or B, Saigon-era) — survived; mild residual hepatic findings would be expected but Formula appears to have ameliorated.
- Torture sequelae: captured at least twice in this period (briefly each time). Documented healed cigarette burns on left ventral forearm in a deliberate triangular array (visible in art, attributed by Ennis to a Soviet GRU interrogation, 1956). Healed scalpel scars at the left flank and right axilla, consistent with controlled pain-administration rather than combat. He has never referenced these aloud in canon.
- Soft-tissue knife injuries — at least three significant lacerations across this period, including a defensive wound across the right palm that limits a tendon's full excursion by perhaps 5° at full extension. Not functionally significant; visible in close art.
- Continued retention of WWII shrapnel.
- **Onset of established cigar habit** — by the late 1940s the cigar is fixed as instrument and prop. See §2.7.

**Notable absences:** no documented alcohol-related medical event despite operational immersion in a culture saturated with it. He drinks; he does not drink to medical consequence on the record. This is itself diagnostic — see §3.

---

## 2.5 S.H.I.E.L.D. Directorship Era — The Modern Acute Record (1965–c. 2004)

The Steranko-through-Hickman period is the longest continuous operational stretch of Fury's life and the period in which his body is most often imaged in canon.

**Major somatic events, era:**
- **Deathlok-adjacent reconstructive episode** (per various dossier reconstructions): no canonical full-body cybernetic conversion of Fury, but multiple emergency interventions involving experimental S.H.I.E.L.D. medical assets. Fury has been the patient on the table of the same medical division that builds Life Model Decoys; this fact alone has had to be metabolized somewhere in his psyche.
- **LMD interface phenomena.** Throughout the Steranko run and after, Fury is repeatedly impersonated by Life Model Decoys; on at least two depicted occasions he has been uncertain in the moment whether he was the original or a copy. This is not a medical event in the classical sense — *but it is a somatic-identity event.* The lived experience of not being epistemologically certain that your body is the original is, in clinical terms, an iatrogenic depersonalization-spectrum exposure. He has been exposed to this stimulus dozens of times. Effects on long-term self-experience: nontrivial; under-examined by him.
- Repeated zero-G and high-G exposure (Helicarrier and orbital operations). No documented long-term vestibular damage.
- Exposure to A.I.M. and HYDRA bioweapon prototypes on multiple occasions; in at least one instance (Steranko-era "Death-Spore" arc, in spirit) he was the index case for an antidote race against his own clock. Survived.
- Cumulative blast/concussive exposure continues; cumulative GSW count continues to rise; cumulative laceration count continues to rise.
- **Cardiovascular fitness:** maintained at elite level. Fury runs, lifts, spars, and shoots to maintenance standard well into the chronological 9th and 10th decades — sustained by Formula plus discipline. He does not skip this work. It is one of the very few rituals he has never broken.
- **Surgeries:** appendectomy (uncertain date, likely 1950s, transverse RLQ scar visible). At least one exploratory laparotomy for abdominal GSW with hollow-viscus injury (midline scar, visible in shirtless art, Hitch *Ultimates* era, modernized but consistent with the lineage). Multiple debridements. No joint replacements (Formula).
- **Skin:** moderate actinic damage from decades of outdoor operational exposure, partially masked by complexion and now by Formula-arrested age. Several small benign lesions present and ignored.
- **Hearing:** chronic high-frequency loss with persistent tinnitus, bilateral, worse on the right (the side closer to most of his rifle reports given monocular setup forces the rifle to the right shoulder). Documented across the record by his habit of leaning in or repositioning during quiet conversation; he often asks once and then proceeds as if he heard, a recognizable behavioral compensation.

---

## 2.6 *Secret War* through *Original Sin* — Late-Period Somatic Findings (c. 2004–2014)

**Underground years (post-*Secret War*, Bendis 2004–onward):** Fury operates without official medical support. He establishes off-book medical relationships — at least one trauma surgeon and one biochemist on permanent retainer, names withheld even in his own files. Medical supply chain for the Formula in this period becomes precarious; he is depicted at least once in canon visibly aging out at the edges before resupply, which he treats with the same affect he treats a low magazine: an operational problem, addressed.

**"Man on the Wall" period (*Original Sin*, Aaron 2014):** retrospective revelation that for decades Fury has been operating as a unilateral planetary defender. The medically relevant fact is the *physical cost* — the issue prefigures his accelerated aging at the climax. When the secret breaks and the Formula access is functionally severed, he ages on-panel into the chronological body he would otherwise inhabit: gaunt, white-haired, drawn, his actual hundred-plus years made visible. **This sequence is the most important single medical image in the entire file.** It is the body that has been there all along, briefly uncovered.

**The Unseen transformation:** at the close of *Original Sin*, Fury — having killed the Watcher's assailant and absorbed Watcher knowledge — is transformed and bound to the lunar surface as "The Unseen." Somatically: skin altered, eye altered (a new ocular geometry), motility constrained, sensory aperture vastly expanded but action-bandwidth reduced to near zero. The Formula question is moot; the body is no longer on a human metabolic schedule. **Iatrogenic immobilization of a man whose entire identity is action.** The medical fact is the psychological injury. See §3 — this is his hell rendered as anatomy.

---

## 2.7 Substances, Habits, Rituals of the Body

**Tobacco.** The cigar is the single most important non-clothing object on his person across the record. Onset: late 1940s. Frequency: heavy daily across decades. Type: variable — cheap stogies in the field; better leaf in the office; in the Steranko era a recognizable consistent form. Pharmacologically: nicotine dependency, chronic, severe. He has never been depicted seriously attempting cessation. He has been depicted *without* the cigar in moments of extreme gravity — and the absence reads, because the presence is the baseline.

Behaviorally the cigar is not simply an addiction. It is:
- **A paced-breathing instrument.** Drawing on a cigar produces a slow inhalation, hold, and exhalation cycle indistinguishable from clinical breath-regulation. He self-soothes through it.
- **A timing instrument.** He uses the draw and exhale to insert pauses into interrogations and negotiations; he reads opponents in the interval.
- **An olfactory perimeter.** The smell of his cigar precedes him into rooms and lingers after; subordinates orient to it. This is operationally useful and personally chosen.
- **A permitted oral fixation in a man who has no other.** He does not chew gum, bite nails, twirl pens. He has one mouth-ritual and he commits to it.

**Predicted long-term medical sequelae** — laryngeal/oral risk, cardiovascular risk, COPD risk — appear partially blunted by the Formula. *Partially* is the operative word; this is not protection, it is delay. The record does not show him symptomatic. The body that aged on-panel in *Original Sin* was a body that had been smoking for sixty subjective years.

**Alcohol.** Social, moderate, occasionally hard in mourning contexts. No canonical AUD. He drinks neat spirits, brown, and he drinks slowly. He has been visibly drunk in canon perhaps twice. The discipline here is notable in a man of his cohort and exposure — and is itself a finding (the affective constriction that prevents him from properly grieving also prevents him from properly self-medicating).

**Caffeine.** Continuous, military-grade, indifferent to vehicle (coffee, the worst available; tea under British operational cover; whatever's hot).

**Sleep.** Chronically partial. Depicted sleeping at desks, on transports, in operations centers, in field positions. Almost never depicted in a domestic bed. The bed, when shown, is unmade and unaccompanied. Sleep architecture is almost certainly fragmented; his ability to function on this baseline is at least partly Formula-mediated and partly the trained skill of a man who has slept in foxholes since he was 22.

**Diet.** Indifferent. Field rations for decades; canteen food; whatever is at the meeting. He eats fast, finishes, and pushes the plate. He does not cook on the record. No food appears to give him pleasure on the record except possibly cigar-and-coffee in the early morning of an operational day.

**Exercise.** Disciplined, daily, lifelong. The one ritual of self-maintenance he has never failed.

**Other substances:** no recreational drug use on the record. Iatrogenic exposure to A.I.M./HYDRA agents during operational captivity, variously, with no documented long-term sequelae the Formula has not absorbed.

---

## 2.8 Disabilities — Functional and Compensated

- **Monocular vision, permanent.** Compensated via behavioral repositioning, technology saturation of operational environments, and preference for elevated/cornered postures. He drives, he shoots, he flies — competently — with the deficit. He will not be the marksman at extreme range that a binocular operator can be. He compensates by closing distance.
- **High-frequency hearing loss with chronic tinnitus.** Compensated by behavioral lean-in, lip-reading skill acquired without formal training, and refusal to admit the deficit aloud.
- **Chronic musculoskeletal compensations** — right cervical/trapezius load from head-turning, lumbar shrapnel-adjacent intermittent pain, old hand fractures producing a slight grip-strength asymmetry (R > L by a small margin). All managed by training and ignored by report.
- **MRI contraindication** from retained ferrous fragments. He requires CT or ultrasound for any imaging study and the medical personnel who know this is a small list.
- **Dental:** maintained adequately; the gold crown referenced above; some attrition consistent with decades of stress-clenching (he grinds at night, inferable from masseter hypertrophy visible in art).

**He does not consider himself disabled.** The patch is not, in his self-concept, a disability marker; it is an identity marker. Any framing that approaches the former produces immediate withdrawal or hostility (interrogation note).

---

## 2.9 Psychological Sequelae of the Medical Record — Summary

Each somatic insult has a psychological residue, and the residues are stacked in a particular order that produces the personality §3 will describe in detail. Briefly enumerated here:

- **The eye** is the conversion point at which an injury became an identity


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT N.J. FURY

*Compiled from cross-decade observational record, surveillance composites, medical reconstructions, and inferential extrapolation from canonical depiction (Kirby, Steranko, Chaykin, Hitch, Maleev, Deodato, Hitch, Hickman/Caselli, Aaron/Deodato, Ennis/Parlov).*

---

## I. GROSS PHYSICAL BASELINE

**Build.** Heavyweight middleweight in old boxing terms: roughly 6'0", 220 lbs of dry mass, ratio shifted toward upper-body and posterior-chain musculature consistent with a man who has done seventy-plus years of unloaded calisthenics, sandbag work, and grappling rather than barbell hypertrophy. Trapezius and lateral neck development are pronounced — the residue of decades of carrying a head turned constantly to compensate for a missing visual hemisphere. Forearm and grip development disproportionate to upper arm: the body of a man who has held people and weapons more than he has lifted weights for display.

**Skin.** Weathered Black skin with sun-thickening at the temples, the back of the neck, and the dorsum of both hands; cold-cracked knuckles year-round; a permanent slight darkening across the bridge of the nose where the patch strap rides. Visible scarring inventory, partial: a comma-shaped scar above the right eyebrow (rifle butt, depicted Steranko era); a puckered entry-and-exit pair high on the left deltoid (small-caliber, through-and-through, healed without proper debridement); a shrapnel-scatter constellation across the lower abdomen and right iliac crest (the grenade, France, 1944 — the same explosion that took the eye); a long, fine surgical line along the medial right thigh (femoral repair, undated); blade-scar across the inside of the left forearm where he learned, once, not to block with the radial side; cigar burns on the back of the left wrist that are not accidents — old self-administered tells to stay awake on long surveillance.

**The eye.** Left orbit: globe present, non-functional, scarred cornea and disorganized iris visible to anyone permitted to see it (almost no one is). The patch is a flat black elastic over a soft leather cup, replaced approximately twice yearly, always identical model — a tradecraft constant. The strap rides a millimeter higher on the right (the asymmetry has marked the skin). He has refused, on the documented record, three separate prosthetic and three separate regenerative-tissue options. **Inferred:** the wound is not a thing he is healing from; it is a thing he is keeping.

**Hair and grooming.** Hair worn close-cropped to the scalp since the mid-1940s; tolerates approximately three weeks before re-cut; performs the cut himself with electric clippers in roughly four minutes in front of a mirror without sentiment. Facial hair: a goatee maintained in the modern era at a length that requires daily attention but presents as careless — the deliberate construction of a man who does not want to appear groomed. He shaves the cheeks and neck with a straight razor when possible, safety razor in the field, never electric — a habit dating to a period in the 1950s when he did not trust electrics not to be bugged and never updated. Nails kept very short, filed not clipped, edges blunt — operational consideration (a clipped edge can snag on a holster, a glove, a person's skin). No cologne, ever. Soap: institutional bar soap, scent-neutral.

## II. POSTURE, STANCE, AND THE GEOMETRY OF THE ROOM

**Standing baseline.** Weight 60/40 on the back foot, hips squared but shoulders slightly bladed to whoever he is talking to so the dead eye is presented rather than the live one — an inversion of intuitive practice that puts his good field where threats are statistically more likely to emerge (the door, the room at large) rather than on the person he is addressing. Hands: rarely in pockets, never both at once. The non-dominant hand is usually doing something small (cigar, coffee cup, the edge of a folder, a coin) — occupying itself so the dominant hand can stay free.

**Seated.** Will not sit with his back to a door. In any room with more than one entrance he will reposition the chair, with no comment, before sitting. In rooms where this is impossible (briefings, others' offices), he stands. He has been documented standing through ninety-minute meetings in the Pentagon and the Triskelion rather than accept a chair facing the wrong way. When he must sit facing wrong, the right hand drops out of sight below the desk line and rests on his thigh near where a sidearm would be — present whether the sidearm is or not.

**Spatial preference.** Elevated and corner positions, consistent across artists and decades: catwalks in hangar bays, the upper deck of bridges, the back booth in any restaurant, the second-floor window when standing watch. In a tactical operations center he positions himself at the rear of the room facing the screens, never at the front facing the personnel — surveils the watchers and the watched simultaneously.

**Gait.** Heel-strike forward, slightly rolling, economical — a walk that eats ground without appearing to hurry. Step length shortens noticeably on his blind side when entering unfamiliar interiors; he is shortening his commitment so he can pivot. On stairs: descends with the right hand free of the rail, ascends taking two at a time when alone, one at a time when accompanied. Will not walk in step with a partner — breaks cadence within three or four paces, an old habit against synchronized targeting.

**The head-turn.** The single most diagnostic motor pattern. Approximately every six to nine seconds in any unsecured environment, his head executes a small left-rotation of perhaps twenty degrees, holds for under a second, returns. He is sweeping the dead field. In high-threat environments the interval drops to three or four seconds. In intimate or fully secured environments (rare) it lengthens to twenty or thirty seconds but never disappears. He himself is no longer aware of doing it.

## III. THE FACE

**Resting expression.** Slight frown — a tonic contraction of the corrugator complex that has, over decades, etched two vertical lines between the brows and a single transverse line at the bridge of the nose. The mouth at rest is closed, lips firm but not pressed, jaw very slightly clenched (masseter hypertrophy visible in profile). The good eye is narrowed perhaps fifteen percent off neutral — a man perpetually reading middle distance.

**The smile, when it appears.** Asymmetric, right side higher (the side with the eye that participates). Brief — rarely held more than a second and a half. Two registers: a closed-lip flicker that signals genuine private amusement, generally directed at irony rather than humor, and a fuller open smile, teeth visible, reserved almost exclusively for the small circle (Dugan, Jones, the rare moment with the Contessa or with Daisy Johnson) and for misdirection in tradecraft — the "everything is fine here" smile he wears when something is not.

**The laugh.** A single exhaled syllable through the nose, often: "Hmph." Full laughter — chest, audible — is documented perhaps a dozen times across six decades of record, all of them in the company of Dugan, all of them after combat, all of them brief.

**Eye behavior (the live one).** Blink rate suppressed below population baseline in operational settings — approximately eight to ten per minute against a norm of fifteen to twenty. He has trained out the involuntary blink-on-startle, which gives interlocutors the disconcerting sense that he sees things they don't react to. Pupillary response intact and brisk. When listening hard he tilts the head slightly to bring the live eye more squarely on the speaker's mouth as much as on their eyes — he reads lips by habit even when not needing to.

**Micro-expressions.** Anger leaks first at the nostrils (flare of less than a millimeter, briefly held). Disgust at the upper lip on the live-eye side. Surprise — when he permits it — at the eyebrow on the live-eye side only; the dead side does not move much, the corrugator there having weakened with decades of disuse. Sadness almost never reaches the face; when it does, it is a single slow blink and a turn of the head away.

## IV. HANDS AND THE CIGAR

**Hand baseline.** Large, calloused along the ulnar edge (sword-edge of the hand — the surface he hits with), thickened pads on the trigger finger and on the web between thumb and index. The right hand has a slight resting tremor under fatigue, noticeable only when he holds a coffee cup at chest height; he steadies it by transferring to the left or by setting it down. Both hands run perpetually warm; he does not wear gloves indoors.

**The cigar.** The single most over-determined object in his somatic life. Always held in the left hand when not being smoked — keeps the right free. Lit with a battered Zippo (not a lighter brand he chose; a lighter he kept) using a three-strike maximum: if it doesn't catch in three, he closes the lighter and waits, refusing to look as though he is fumbling. The cigar serves at least six discrete functions and shifts among them by state:

- **Pacing breath under stress** — drawn slowly, exhaled through the nose in a six-count, a self-administered vagal brake disguised as a habit.
- **Buying time in conversation** — a draw and a deliberate exhale fills three to five seconds in which he is constructing the next sentence or waiting for the other person to fill the silence.
- **Establishing dominance over physical space** — the smoke encroaches without his having to.
- **Olfactory disruption** — masks his own scent signature, masks the room's.
- **Concealing the mouth** — held at the lips, it covers half the face during difficult disclosures.
- **A weapon of last resort** — twice in the canonical record, used as an improvised burn against a grappling opponent's hand or eye.

Cigar consumption rises sharply in pre-operational planning, falls during active operations (he will not smoke on infiltration), and rises again in after-action. He does not smoke in the presence of children or non-consenting subordinates and is meticulous about this in a way he is meticulous about little else.

**Gesture inventory.** Talks with his hands minimally; the right hand will rise to chest height to make a single point, settle. Points with the cigar, never the finger, when addressing a group. When listening, the right hand often comes up to the jaw — thumb under the chin, index along the cheek toward the live eye — a posture that incidentally guards the throat and partially shields the lip-read. Under intense focus he taps the index finger of the right hand against the surface he is touching, a slow one-per-second metronome that is not nervousness but timing.

## V. VOICE AND SPEECH

**Baseline voice.** Low chest register, gravel from decades of cigars and shouting, projects without effort. Speaks more quietly than people expect — he learned early that lowering volume makes a room lean in. Articulation crisp; a faint residual New York consonant pattern (the cleaner-than-stereotype Hell's Kitchen vowels of a man who long ago made command-level English a deliberate acquisition over street English).

**Profanity.** Constant, structural, and rhythmically musical — not decorative. Functions as: tension regulator, register-setter (signals "we are at work now, not at court"), and class assertion (he refuses, across seven decades, to be made into an officer's accent). Profanity rate is highest in moderate-stress operational settings and *drops* under acute threat — when things actually go bad his speech becomes clipped, declarative, profanity-free.

**Speech under state shift.**
- *Calm/private:* slower, longer phrases, dry humor, complete sentences, occasional storytelling.
- *Operational/normal stress:* compressed, profane, imperative mood, callsigns rather than names.
- *Acute threat:* monosyllabic, present-tense, no profanity, voice drops further in pitch, breath audible between phrases.
- *Intimate:* near-whisper, single-word affirmatives, long pauses; he will go entire minutes without speaking and not feel the absence.
- *Lying to a friend for their own good:* the cadence flattens, the eye contact intensifies past his own baseline (overcorrection), the cigar moves to cover the mouth.

## VI. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Total sleep time:** estimated four to five hours in any twenty-four-hour cycle, polyphasic. The Infinity Formula appears to reduce required sleep modestly but not to eliminate it; he has been observed in micro-sleeps (under ninety seconds, eyes-open variants) on long transports.

**Position.** Sleeps on his right side — the dead-eye side down, the live-eye side toward the room. This is deliberate and lifelong since the wound: he wakes facing whatever is coming. Sleeps with a sidearm within twelve inches of the dominant hand; field expedient versions when no sidearm is available involve a knife under the pillow or a chair wedged under the doorknob, a habit he cannot turn off in hotel rooms even in fully secured environments.

**Sleep onset.** Rapid (under three minutes) in any environment he has personally cleared; protracted (forty minutes or more) in environments cleared by others. He does not read or watch to fall asleep; he simply closes the live eye and is gone or is not.

**Wake.** Wakes fully and instantly — there is no transitional grogginess on the record. The first motor act is the right hand to the weapon, completed before the eye opens; the second is the eye opening; the third is the head turn left to clear the dead field. The whole sequence is sub-two-seconds and has been observed by every author who has put him in a bed.

**Dreams.** Not directly accessible from the record. Inferable from behavior: he has been depicted, in the Ennis material and in late Aaron, waking with a hand already at the throat (own or imagined other's), suggesting at minimum strangulation/proximity-violence motifs. He does not speak of dreams. Does not journal. Does not report to anyone.

## VII. EATING AND DRINKING

**Pattern.** Functional, not pleasurable. Eats fast when alone (a meal in under seven minutes, head down, scanning between bites), slowly when with the small circle (will linger over a meal with Dugan in a way he will do for almost no other reason). Standing meals more common than seated. Will eat almost anything; specifically documented preferences: black coffee (constant, large quantities, takes it scalding); rye whiskey neat (rare, ritualized — usually in the company of one specific person and usually marking a death); diner-grade breakfast food at any hour; cured meats and hard cheese as field rations of preference. **Has been observed to refuse food only when poisoning is plausible** — does not eat from buffets in non-cleared locations, will not accept a drink he did not see poured.

**Hydration.** Underhydrated by clinical standards; treats water as something to manage thirst with rather than a regular intake. Coffee functions as primary fluid.

**The whiskey ritual.** Two fingers, neat, in a heavy-bottomed glass; lifted, held briefly at chest height (a beat of silent acknowledgment that is the closest he gets to prayer for the dead), then drunk in two pulls, not one. Pours a second only if the company stays.

## VIII. SEXUALITY AND INTIMACY

**Behavioral pattern across record.** Heterosexual on the depicted evidence; capable of intense, focused attention on a partner during the windows he is present; structurally incapable of staying through the morning more than a handful of times in any given relationship. Lovers consistently describe (in the Ennis-era depictions and others) the same paradox: he is more present in two hours than most men are in two years, and then he is gone for months.

**Physical conduct in intimate settings.** Slower than expected — he reads the room/body the way he reads operational environments, with attention to micro-signal. The patch comes off only with specific partners and only after a window of trust; the act of removing it is itself a disclosure heavier than the disrobing. He prefers to be touched on the live-eye side of the face; flinches very slightly when touched on the dead side, has trained the flinch down but has not eliminated it.

**Post-coital pattern.** Smokes, eventually sleeps if the environment is cleared, leaves before the partner wakes more often than not. The leaving is not avoidant in the casual sense; it is operational hygiene that has become character.

**Affective tells in intimacy.** The voice drops further than its baseline drop; the profanity disappears entirely; he uses the partner's name more than he uses any name in any other context, as though pinning the moment.

## IX. GROOMING, DRESS, AND OBJECTS ON THE BODY

**Wardrobe.** Functional, dark, minimal palette — black, charcoal, olive, occasional navy. Wears tactical when tactical is called for and a quiet suit when a suit is called for; equally at home in both and at home in neither. Will not wear white (laundry tells, visibility). Boots over shoes by a wide margin; the boots are broken-in to the point of being part of the foot; he resoles rather than replaces.

**Constant carry.** Sidearm (model has shifted across eras, preference for reliable over exotic); backup blade at the small of the back or in the boot; the Zippo; cigars in a slim metal case in the inside breast pocket (the case has stopped at least one bullet in the canon); a small notebook and a stub pencil — he writes in shorthand of his own devising, never in pen (pen smears under blood, water, sweat); a single key on a leather thong that opens something nobody has ever asked him about.

**Watch.** Wears a watch on the right wrist (he is right-dominant; this is unusual and deliberate — keeps the dominant wrist unencumbered for the draw, the watch on the support side). The watch is mechanical, wound by hand each morning in a thirty-second ritual that doubles as a daily orientation in time he is structurally adrift from.

## X. MICRO-MOVEMENT TELLS AND STATE TRANSITIONS

**Tells of escalating concern (in order of appearance):**
1. The head-turn interval shortens.
2. The cigar comes out and is held but not lit.
3. The right hand drifts to the hip or the small of the back.
4. The voice quiets.
5. The profanity drops away.
6. He moves, without announcement, to a position from which he can see the door and an exit other than the door.
7. He sends the nearest person he cares about out of the room on a pretext.

**Tells of grief (rare, brief, easily missed):**
- A single long exhale through the nose, longer than his cigar-exhale.
- The live eye closes for approximately two seconds — not a blink, a closure.
- The right hand goes flat against a surface — table, wall, a coffin lid — and stays for a count of three.
- He leaves the room. He does not return to that room that day.

**Tells of moral injury active (the deepest tell, hardest to read):**
- He becomes unusually solicitous in small ways — pours someone else's coffee, holds a door, asks after a subordinate's family — overcorrecting toward the human in compensation for a decision he has just made or is about to make against the human.
- He smokes faster.
- He sleeps less that night, and is harder than usual the following morning.

**Tells of intimacy permitted:**
- The patch strap loosens (he adjusts it down a quarter inch, an unconscious release).
- The shoulders drop perhaps two centimeters.
- The cigar gets set down rather than held.
- He uses the other person's first name in a complete sentence.
- He sits with his back to a door he has not personally cleared. This last is, in the entire surveillance composite, the single most reliable indicator that the person he is with has been admitted to a circle of perhaps four living people on the planet.

---

*End of Somatic Atlas. Cross-reference: Sections on Routes & Rituals, Tradecraft Signature, and Relational Mapping for behavioral signatures embedded in movement, communication, and contact patterns.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## Subject: Fury, N.J. — Section 6 of the Longitudinal Workup

---

## 6.1 The Originating Template: A Secure-Anxious Substrate, Built on an Absence

The clinical mistake to avoid, with this subject, is to read the late-career flatness backward and conclude he was always cold. The published record contradicts this. The young Sergeant Fury of the 1940s — the man on the Howling Commandos record — was an unusually **warm, communal, somatically affectionate** organizer of male attachment. He grabbed shoulders. He shoved chests in affection. He sat closer to his men than rank required. He learned every Commando's family situation and remembered it under fire. This is not the behavior of a constitutionally avoidant person; this is the behavior of someone whose first attachment system was **wired for fierce in-group bonding** and whose adult relational style was, at baseline, what attachment researchers would call **secure with an anxious lean** — capable of trust, prone to over-investment, vulnerable to loss.

The origin material explains the lean. The father — a WWI aviator killed when the subject was very young — is the single most determining absence in the file. The subject inherits a **heroic male template that he cannot interrogate**, because the template never made it home to be human at the breakfast table. The mother is not depicted in canon at all, which is itself a clinical datum: the subject does not narrate her, does not invoke her, does not visit her grave on the record. Whether her absence reflects loss, estrangement, or merely the silence of mid-century working-class Irish Catholic emotional culture, the result is the same — the subject grew up with **no on-the-record adult who modeled the soft side of attachment**, no observed dyad of mutual care to template from. He has a brother (Jacob) whose existence is largely shadow material, weaponized later by villains; the sibling bond is structurally significant by its discontinuity.

What he had instead were **streets, fistfights, and the substitute brotherhood of any group of working-class boys that would have him**. The bond he learned to make is the bond of *shared physical risk*. This is the only intimacy template he ever fully metabolized, and it is the template he reproduces, in deteriorating form, for the next eighty years.

---

## 6.2 The Howling Commandos Era: Attachment at Full Voltage

This is the only period in the entire published record in which the subject's attachment system operates at full capacity, in real time, with appropriate object and appropriate reciprocity. Granular pattern:

- **He learns the men's tells.** He knows which Commando flinches at artillery (Juniper), which one talks through fear (Dugan), which one goes silent (Gabe Jones), which one performs unconcern (Pinkerton). He calibrates his command voice individually. Surveillance-grade observation: across the Lee/Kirby and Ayers runs, he is depicted positioning himself **bodily between specific men and specific threats** in a manner that varies by Commando — covering Jones in firefights more often than statistical chance would dictate, putting Dugan on his right where his blind side will eventually be.
- **He fights his own command structure for them.** The Gabe Jones segregation confrontation (*Sgt. Fury* #1, 1963) is not a one-off. He is repeatedly written as a man who will accept punishment from above to spare a Commando from above. This is the single behavior that defines his relationship to all hierarchy thereafter: **chain of command is a thing he uses, not a thing he obeys, when his people are at stake.**
- **He cannot adequately mourn Juniper.** Jonathan Juniper's death in the early arc is the first textualized in-group loss. The subject's processing of it on the page is a **single beat of grief followed by tactical re-deployment**. This is not yet pathology — it is wartime command — but the *shape* of his lifelong grief response is already visible: register, displace, work harder. The pattern, once established under combat conditions where it was adaptive, will never be modified, even when context changes.
- **Lady Pamela Hawley** (*Sgt. Fury* #18) is the first adult romantic attachment on record and the first that exposes the structural vulnerability. He loved her clearly, courted her with discomfort because the register was wrong for him, and lost her to the Blitz. **He returns to the unit and does not speak of her again at depth.** The work absorbs the grief. He will repeat this exact maneuver, with diminishing affective availability, with every subsequent female partner.

The Howlers are the **only relational structure in his life that he did not eventually betray, deceive, or instrumentally use**. They are the floor. Every later relationship is measured, by him, against that floor — and found wanting, and treated accordingly.

---

## 6.3 The Cold War Decades: The Acquisition of Operational Cynicism Without Moral Collapse

Across the late 40s through the 60s (Ennis, *Fury: My War Gone By*), the subject's relational system undergoes a transformation that is best described as the **slow conversion of warmth into watchfulness**. The behavioral indicators:

- **Shirley Defabio.** Long-running, adulterous, structurally impossible. She is married; he is gone for months at a time; the affair persists for years and is abandoned. What the file should note: he chose, twice, a woman he could not have, *first* (Hawley, separated by war and class) and *second* (Defabio, separated by marriage and absence). **The pattern is choosing intimacy structured to fail.** This is not yet conscious; it will become so.
- **Larry Hama (later) and the CIA mentors of this era.** He learns from men who have already made the trade he is making. He watches them die badly, or live worse. The lesson he extracts is not "do not become this" but "become this with eyes open."
- **He begins to lie to friends in their interest.** The first textualized instances of withholding mission-relevant information from teammates date to this period. Each individual instance is defensible. The cumulative drift is not.

By the time he is recruited to S.H.I.E.L.D., the **attachment system is intact but rerouted through operational logic**. He loves the men he loves; he simply structures his relationships so that the love does not impede the work.

---

## 6.4 The S.H.I.E.L.D. Decades and the Contessa: The Last Real Attempt

Contessa Valentina Allegra de Fontaine is the **most documented late-career intimate**. She enters the record in *Strange Tales* #142 (Steranko, 1966) and persists, intermittently, across decades. The relationship's longitudinal shape is diagnostically rich:

- **Initial register: bantering, combative, sexually charged, professionally peer.** He likes that she does not fold. The chemistry depicted is real and mutual.
- **Middle register: chronic intermittence.** They are together when missions converge; apart when missions diverge; she is repeatedly written as the one who pushes for more presence, he as the one who deflects with operational necessity. **This is the canonical avoidant-pursuer dynamic, with him on the avoidant pole — a pole he did not occupy in the Howling Commandos era.** The Formula years have done their work.
- **Late register: she becomes a HYDRA double in some continuities, an antagonist in others.** The betrayal arcs — whichever continuity — are not just plot. They are the **canonical confirmation of the subject's worst working hypothesis**: that even the women he loves can be enemy assets, that intimacy is an intelligence vulnerability, that the only safe attachment is the one held at distance.

After Val, **there is no replacement**. The record contains flirtations, single nights, operational alliances with affective overtones — but no sustained adult intimate partnership is depicted with anything like the Val arc's investment. The subject has, functionally, **retired from the partnered intimate domain** by the late 1980s in publication time, and the retirement has held.

---

## 6.5 The Dugan Exception: The Only Relationship That Survives the Math

Timothy "Dum Dum" Dugan is the structurally singular relationship in the file. The reason is pharmacological and the consequence is psychological. Dugan also receives the Infinity Formula. **Dugan is the only person in the subject's life who is not aging out of him.**

The behavioral effects are observable across decades:

- **Dugan is the only person to whom the subject reliably tells the truth.** Not the whole truth — Fury does not tell anyone the whole truth — but the **operational truth he tells no one else**. The compartmentalization that defines every other relationship is, with Dugan, relaxed by perhaps 30%.
- **Physical proximity in panel composition.** Across artists from Kirby to Steranko to Hitch to Deodato, the subject is reliably positioned **at Dugan's flank** — Dugan on his blind side as often as his sighted side, which is an extraordinary statement of trust from a monocular operator who prefers overwatch positions.
- **The humor register relaxes.** The dry, dark, intact humor is broader and looser with Dugan than with anyone else.
- **He has, repeatedly, broken protocol to extract Dugan personally from situations he would have delegated for anyone else.**
- **And — the diagnostic tell — he does not say what Dugan means to him.** Even here. Even with the man who has been beside him for eighty years. The most secure attachment in his adult life is conducted in the register of shoulder-grabs, shared cigars, and operational reliability. The words have never come.

Dugan-related arcs (especially the LMD/HYDRA revelations of the Hickman era and the later Aaron material) are the moments at which the subject's affective armor is most likely to crack on the page, and they crack only briefly, and they reseal.

---

## 6.6 The Mentorship Pattern: Paternal in the Older Military Mode

The subject is a serial mentor and a serial disappointment to mentees, in a specific pattern:

- **Phil Coulson.** Loyal, durable, drawn into the work, kept at one ring of compartmentalization out from the inner truth. The subject withholds mission-stakes information from Coulson on multiple occasions, in the conviction that the withholding is protective. Coulson reads this, correctly, as both care and condescension.
- **Daisy Johnson / Quake.** The closest thing to a successor the subject has produced. Recruited young, trained personally, made head of the Caterpillars in the Hickman run. The subject's mentorship of her is **the closest he has come, in the modern era, to admitting he is grooming a replacement** — and the *Secret Warriors* arc shows him sending her into operational situations whose full stakes he conceals. He cares; he lies; he gets her wounded; he repeats. She loves him; she also leaves.
- **The Secret Warriors writ large.** He recruits the children of supervillains and superheroes and trains them. The pattern: **paternal warmth in the field, paternal absence in the meaning, paternal deception about the larger frame.** When the frame is revealed (HYDRA inside S.H.I.E.L.D. all along), several of them die before he can extract them. He absorbs this and does not show it.
- **Nick Fury Jr.** The biological son. The relationship is canonically distant, transactional, and **the most direct repetition of the absent-aviator-father template** in the file. He cannot give the boy what he himself never received, because he has no model for it. He gives instead what he does have: tradecraft, opportunity, and the assumption that the son will figure out the love on his own.

The mentorship template, repeated across every iteration: **draw close, train hard, withhold the frame, send into harm, absorb the loss, do not say what they meant.**

---

## 6.7 Peer Relationships: Wary Respect, Strategic Deception, Accepted Cost

With peers — Steve Rogers, Tony Stark, Charles Xavier, T'Challa, the senior cape community generally — the subject runs a consistent program:

- **Public respect, real and reciprocated.**
- **Private willingness to deceive them in what he assesses to be their interest.** Bendis's *Secret War* is the canonical instance, but the behavior is older and broader.
- **Acceptance of the relationship cost when the deception is exposed.** He does not apologize, in the integrative sense. He explains the assessment, accepts the rupture, and continues to operate on the same premise the next time.

The relationship with **Steve Rogers** is the diagnostic case. Rogers is one of perhaps three people in the subject's life with the moral standing to call him on his methods — and the subject, in every arc, **arranges his interactions with Rogers to minimize the moments Rogers could so call him.** He briefs Rogers selectively. He activates Rogers late. He sends Rogers in for the operations Rogers will approve of and runs the others without him. This is not contempt; it is a specific form of **respect that cannot tolerate being judged by the respected party.** He protects the relationship by hollowing it.

---

## 6.8 The Mechanism of Distrust: Pattern-Matching to an Eighty-Year Dataset

The subject's distrust is not paranoid in the clinical sense and not free-floating. It is **empirically calibrated to a dataset no one else has had time to accumulate.** He has personally watched: the OSS become the CIA become a thing that kills its own; S.H.I.E.L.D. be a HYDRA front from its founding (Hickman); the U.S. government refuse action on threats it later was destroyed by; allies turn out to be Skrulls (Bendis, *Secret Invasion*); doubles of himself act in his name; the Watcher fail at watching. His baseline assumption that institutions are penetrated by default is **the correct Bayesian read on his observed evidence.**

The relational consequence is severe: he extends provisional trust quickly (operational necessity) and unconditional trust almost never. The category of unconditional trust contains, as of the latest material, perhaps **two living names**.

---

## 6.9 The Mechanism of Betrayal: Always "For Their Own Good"

The subject is a betrayer. The file must be honest about this. He has, on the record:

- Lied to teammates about operational stakes (*Secret War*, repeatedly elsewhere).
- Run parallel intelligence services hidden from the institution he led (*Secret Warriors*).
